  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1b29be26-cff6-4e0f-9d40-265d86078822'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText9867264163531938600" style="display:none"><i>The final book in The Original Sinners Series - The Red Years.</i><br /><br />There's punishment-and then there's vengeance.<br /><br />Nora Sutherlin is being held, bound and naked. Under different circumstances, she would enjoy the situation immensely, but her captor isn't interested in play. Or pity.<br /><br />As the reality of her impending peril unfolds, Nora becomes Scheherazade, buying each hour of her life with stories-sensual tales of Søren, Kingsley and Wesley, each of whom has tempted and tested and tortured her in his own way. This, Nora realizes, is her life: nothing so simple, so vanilla, as a mere love triangle for her. It's a knot in a silken cord, a tangled mass of longings of the body and the heart and the mind. And it may unravel at any moment.<br /><br />But in Nora's world, no one is ever truly powerless-a cadre of her friends, protectors and lovers stands ready to do anything to save her, even when the only certainty seems to be sacrifice and heartbreak....</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1257592171" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9111105214364850814"><b> ::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: </b><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429411092i/14584535.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><strong>WHAT. A. BOOK!!!</strong><br/><br/>First before anything.... I have to say: <strong>#TeamSøren </strong><br/><br/>Omg, so completely, utterly, and irrevocably #TeamSøren.<br/>(Lol, apparently I'm a switch. WAY!!!!<br/><br/>My feels have been toyed with, my mind has been fucked with, my emotions are now so tangled up that I went from being a 100% solid #TeamWesley gal, to being so completely on #TeamSøren that it's hard for me to accept that I was ever </span>
  <span id="freeText9111105214364850814" style="display:none"><b> ::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: </b><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429411092i/14584535.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><strong>WHAT. A. BOOK!!!</strong><br><br>First before anything.... I have to say: <strong>#TeamSøren </strong><br><br>Omg, so completely, utterly, and irrevocably #TeamSøren.<br>(Lol, apparently I'm a switch. Hehe. Get it? ;) )<br>Gah. My poor heart!!! But just... <strong>#TEAMSOREN </strong><br><br>ALL. THE. WAY!!!!<br><br>My feels have been toyed with, my mind has been fucked with, my emotions are now so tangled up that I went from being a 100% solid #TeamWesley gal, to being so completely on #TeamSøren that it's hard for me to accept that I was ever <em>not </em>on his team. I honestly didn't believe this would happen. I kept seeing everyone all in love with Søren while I was just eyeing his warily but NOW I GET IT!!! I really do!!<br><br>Please be sure to read the first 3 books in the series (or at least my reviews of them) before reading this because... this book isn't a standalone and I think you should have least the tiniest bit of context. So first check out <a href="http://amzn.to/1ggdK11" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Siren</a> (<a href="http://aestasbookblog.com/the-siren-review/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">my review</a>), <a href="http://amzn.to/1ChNBrW" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Angel</a> (<a href="http://aestasbookblog.com/the-angel-review/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">my review</a>), and <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B0092MLCNQ/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;creativeASIN=B0092MLCNQ&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=aesbooblo-20" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Prince</a> (<a href="http://aestasbookblog.com/the-prince-review/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">my review</a>), m'kay?<br><br>OK. On to the review.<br><br>First things first: THE. WRITING. IS. BRILLIANT!!!!!!!!! Literally some of the best I've <em>ever </em>read.<br><br>BRILLIANT.<br>BRILLIANT.<br>BRILLIANT.<br>Just absolutely fucking amazing!<br><br>The story is <em>the </em>most boundary-pushing one I've ever read. You have to understand that I went into this series completely blind (by choice). And by that, I mean that I literally did not know <em>anything!!!</em> I didn't even read the blurbs. Usually when I read a book, I know who ends up with who and the general direction of the storyline (I'm not a fan of surprises) but with this series, because it was already so far outside the box, I decided to just accept whatever it dished out and try to remain as open minded as possible.<br><br>So this book starts off right after the <em>giant freaking heart-stopping cliffhanger</em> that the previous book left us on that threw the world around Nora into full-out crisis mode. It was so powerful to see the way all these characters that we'd gotten to know over the course of the series come together in this desperate time to work together to help Nora. ALL THE FEELS, I tell you. All the feels.<br><br>I'm not going to go into detail on what this crisis is that they're facing but just trust me that it's about as dire, dangerous, and deadly as you can imagine. Everyone's worst nightmare coming to pass.<br><br>I started this book rooting for Nora and Wes (as I had been feeling at the end of the previous book), but I have to say that that little part of me that had started warming up to Søren in <em>The Prince </em>was beginning to grow with every page I read. There was just <em>no denying</em> that Nora and Søren had this kind of soulmate forever-til-the-day-I-die love for each other. But my heart still broke for Kingsley and his unrequited love for Søren. What a heart breaking emotional tangle it was.<br><br>There was such a intricate web of characters, all bound together by some degree of sexual separation (which alone is fascinating if you think about it), but also bound together by varying and differing measures of the deepest love you can imagine. This is the first time <em>ever</em> that a series has presented and used the concept of people genuinely being in love with (and I mean romantically) more than one person in a way that I not only accepted, but also began to believe and understand.<br><br>Oddly enough, some of my favorite scenes in the whole book were Søren's chats with Grace. Grace is the wife of Nora's editor and one of Nora's few female friends it seemed so she was there to help as best she could. The thing is that everyone, other than Nora and Kingsley, was in some way or another terrified of Søren... so I feel like that naturally meant that it was harder to get to know him as a character. But Grace has this kind of calmness to her that just allowed Søren to be <em>himself</em> around her. I almost feel like the way she was around him turned him into a real person if that makes sense. He never treated her with the dominance of the Underground world because she wasn't a part of that, he never had reason to intimidate her because she posed no threat, he didn't have to cause her pain or humiliation because he wasn't trying to sleep with her, she was happily married so there wasn't really any sexual awkwardness between them... and with the thing he held dearest to him in dire jeopardy, he already had everything on the line and she was trustworthy so he genuinely had no reason to hide, there was just no real reason for his walls to be up. So we got to see <em>him. </em>It was the purest form of him as a person that I feel that we'd ever seen so far in the series. No masks or pretences or games. And I loved it. If I had to pin-point the moment that I joined #TeamSøren, that was it. That's when I fell for him, and when I most truly <em>understood</em> his love for Nora.<br><br>At first I hated myself for moving to #TeamSøren. I felt all kinds of weird guilt. Like I was betraying my own emotions. Ohhh, my poor mind was so thoroughly fucked with. No, it wasn't even a mind fuck, it was an emotion fuck. A total feel-tangle. Up became down, everything I thought I felt went right out the window and was replaced with this overpowering knowledge that Søren and Nora <em>belonged</em> together.<br><br>I feel like I want to go back to my previous reviews and erase everything and just replace it with #TeamSøren #TeamSøren #TeamSøren #TeamSøren #TeamSøren  but... that wouldn't be honest. The truth is that reading this series was a journey of discovery. Along the way, I felt different things based on what I knew, what I thought I knew, and the things I thought I wanted for these characters.<br><br>I think I get it though... these characters have so many layers to their histories that as you're reading the series, you can only form opinions on what you know. And up until this point, what I knew led me to be #TeamWesley... but after learning everything that this book showed me, there left no doubt in my mind -- not even a little -- that #TeamSøren was the only team.<br><br>I feel like I've definitely come away from this series with a much deeper understanding and respect for the psychology behind BDSM. I mean, I understood it mechanically and very basically from other books I'd read prior to this... but this series opened my eyes to it in a much different way. For these characters, it wasn't just a game, it was a lifestyle. I just feel like I really understood where they were coming from and what fuelled their desires so much more.<br><br>And OMG. The <em>way</em> the story built up to the climax was so intense!! My heart was <em>racing!! </em>There were a few moment that I even broke right down crying with the sheer beauty of it. I took deep calming breaths. Even took a tiny break but only a little one because I just <em>COULD NOT STOP READING!!!!</em><br><br>Gahhhhh!! <em>Them</em> in that corner at the end. Just wow. There's just no choice there. No teams. Just them.<br><br>Ok now at this point in my review, I've covered the book up until the 85% mark. In the book, this is the conclusion to a big "section" of the book. It has a resolved ending and truly if I had stopped reading at this point, my rating would be a very easy 5+++++ STARS!!!!!!<br><br>But the book went on... and honestly, I had several strong issues with a lot of the things that happened after this point so I feel like I need to separate the book's rating up into 3 parts.<br><br><strong>0 - 85% in the book: 5+++ STARS</strong><br><strong>85 - 98% in the book: 3 stars</strong><br><strong>98 - 100% in the book: I'm just going to pretend this didn't happen</strong><br><br>Ok, there are HUGE SPOILERS in this next part of the review, so I've hidden them. You have to click to open them. If you have not yet read this book, I do <em>not</em> recommend you read them. I've written them more for the other people who have already read these books because I kinda just needed to get my feelings out. If you have not read this book or series yet, I still highly recommend that you DO try it. Enjoy the first 3 books and the first 85% of this one with all your hearts, and take the rest of it with an optional grain of salt, but don't allow my feelings on it to stop you from reading this book because it truly is AMAZING!<br><br>Ok here goes... <em>click the spoiler below to read more...</em><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><br>I'd like to point out that it wasn't so much that I "didn't like" what happened in this part of the book, but more that I felt that the things that happened were complete "out of character" for Søren and Wesley respectively. I genuinely do not believe that either of them would do the things they did in this part of the book, and I have to say that <em>that</em> was what bothered me (more than the actions themselves).<br><br>LAST WARNING: SPOILERS SPOILERS SPOILERS AHEAD!!!!<br><br>Wesley first. Ok, to sum it up, I don't find it all that believable that he would have moved on from Nora <i>that</i> fast. I just don't. I think that the path he went down was probably a really good one for his character and I could really see it being a good thing for both of them, but it just felt abrupt to me. Too sudden, too soon. Just... the whole thing felt really off to me.<br><br>Now Soren. And this is really where the bigger part of my issues lay...<br><br>After three and a half 450-page books of getting to know Søren's character, I can tell you that in my opinion, the character I've come to know <em>would never, ever, EVER</em> have done this action. He's not only more noble than that, he's way the hell smarter than that.<br><br>It's very important to distinguish here that there have been many scenes (like the blood-play scene) that I didn't like and that made me uncomfortable, but that I accepted openly because they made sense and were a believable part of Søren's character. The reason I didn't like THIS scene was because it DID NOT make sense and was not at all a believable action for him to have done.<br><br><strong>HUGE SPOILERS AHEAD</strong>. Seriously, if you haven't read this book, I don't care how curious you are, PLEASE DON'T READ THIS. Trust me. Ok?<br><br>So, we all know Nora and Søren have an open relationship -- admittedly, that idea took me a while to warm up to but I've genuinely come to respect and understand it. The one thing though that has been repeated over and over again in the course of the series is that Søren has only ever willingly shared his body with TWO people: Nora and Kingsley (I'm discounting Elizabeth), despite so many countless opportunities thrown at him. Yes, he has other women who sub for him, but that is to satisfy his need for sadism. He doesn't actually ever have sex with them. There's a separation there. And I've come to respect it. So I get why he'd have Grace sub for him (heck, Nora even set it up) so that I could deal with (even though it felt weird to me because the thing I loved most about Grace and Søren's relationship in this book was that it was almost just a real friendship without sexual interferance, but whatever -- 'be openminded' has been my mantra with these books). It felt off to me, but I tried to accept it. But then HE ACTUALLY HAS SEX WITH HER TOO. What? <i>What? Whaaaaaaaaat??!??!?!</i> The fuck?! He's old enough that he's had the chance to sleep with countless women and he never did, but then he actually has SEX? With <em>her</em>?? HUH?? Why?? Who is this guy and where did the Soren I've come to know go?? I just... *shakes head* ... I couldn't believe it. I didn't believe it. But FINE. Jeez. Whatever. "Be openminded". I tried, I really tried.<br><br>Then we got to the final page and <em>THAT REVEAL?!?!</em> Just no. No. No. No. No. NO. Hell to the fucking NO. I'm sorry, but for so many reasons I just DO NOT believe that he would have EVER allowed that to happen. He's too smart to have had it been an accident. And he cares too much for Nora to have done it without consulting with her first. So just no. I completely reject this part of the story. It was so out of character that I don't believe it happened. This was a harder limit for me than the darkest, kinkiest, most controversial or shocking thing you could ever imagine. I can't accept it. #TeamDenial here.<br><br>For me, The Mistress ended <em>wonderfully</em> at 85%. I'm still counting it as one of my top favorite books because holy God, it was BRILLIANTLY done. If for some reason you haven't yet read this book but still chose to read the spoiler (which I hope to hell you didn't!!!), PLEASE don't let this deter you from reading the book because if you do, you'll be missing out on a seriously epic read!!<br><br>I hope you can believe me when I say that I really did love the book.<br>Lol, I'm just completely rejecting this one part of it.<br><br>I still love Søren. I still love Wesley. I still love Nora. And Kingsley. And everyone! Ok?<br><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br>Regardless of anything in that spoiler though, the fantastic thing is that 0 -- 85% of this book is a whole, solid story (it even ends in such a way and is long enough that you could argue that it feels like a complete book) so I would still whole-heartedly recommend this series as a TOP FAVORITE!!!<br><br>This series really makes you <em>think</em>. It's thrilling, erotic, and this book had the ultimate emotional mindfuck. This is one of those books you just can't put down. I hung on to each word, drinking in every new secret and revelation. I was in awe of how this author wove so many intersecting storylines together and kept me on the edge of my seat always desperate to turn the next page the whole way through.<br><br>The Mistress wraps up The Red Years part of this series. The next four books are called The White Years and they essentially are prequels to The Red Years even though they should be read after. Right now, I'm going to take a little reading break from this series (possibly even waiting until the final book is out in November) and then I'll likely binge-read the last four books together the same as I did with these first four. But I will be back. FOR SURE!!! I love these characters, I love the writing, I love the series, and I absolutely recommend them for anyone who wants something fantastically well written, intensely erotic, and that doesn't play by any of the rules. But rather, it makes it's own... and it comes out on top.<br><br>- Note: THESE MUST BE READ IN ORDER -<br><br>My review of book #1: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1I3176u">http://bit.ly/1I3176u</a><br>My review of book #2: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1JIzQay">http://bit.ly/1JIzQay</a><br>My review of book #3: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1CXMigF">http://bit.ly/1CXMigF</a><br>________________________________________<br><br><b>SERIES READING ORDER: </b><br>Book #1: The Siren <br>Book #2: The Angel<br>Book #3: The Prince<br>Book #4: The Mistress<br>Book #5: The Saint<br>Book #6: The King<br>Book #7: The Virgin<br>Book #8: The Queen<br><br>_______________________________________<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book   <span id="freeText11594637085684902910" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428127i/856387.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>OMG OMG I LOVE IT!!!!!!!Seriously this author is trying to give me a heart attack!!!<br>Tiffany Reisz just has a way of writing…she draws you into her world of sinners and you don't want to left!!<br><br>In this book Nora is being held captive by a psychopath with no mercy Kingsley's sister Marie-Laure...<br>Marie-Laure is furious with Søren....because he broke her heart thirty-years ago...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428127i/856388.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>While Nora entertains Marie-Laure with tales of her own sexual exploits with Søren,Kingsley and Wesley..<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380423625ra/844054.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Søren,Kingsley,Wesley,Zach's wife Grace and Søren's niece Laila knows who has Nora,and where she is being held...The problem is getting her back without anyone being killed. ..<br><br>The set up of this story was like playing a game of chess..everyone was a pawn to the person that took Nora.. The moves were dangerous and one of our Queens will not make it...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428127i/856389.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Starting to read it..I immediately was swept into the intense and infinite love Søren has for Nora....his Little One... <br><br><b>"Why do you love me so much ,you stupid man?"<br> "Because I met you."</b><br><br><b>"I'm your's" she whispered<br> "I always was.Even when I was with someone else..I was always yours."</b><br><br><b>"Don't be afraid" <br> "This life is nothing but one blink of God's eyes.He'll blink<br> again and we'll be back together." </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425472i/849193._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425472i/849194._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Finally I want to say that I am team Soren!!!No matter how hard I try to not like him because he is a sadist in this book I love him!!!He is perfect for Nora!! <br><br><b>"Søren isn’t nice.But he’s good."..."He’s the best man of earth.” </b><br><br>Wesley matured a lot in this book!!I loved seeing Wesley stand up to Soren!Also I like his scenes with Laila :)) <br>The biggest surprise for me in this book was Grace.Some of her parts made me tear up!<br> <br>I was extremely happy with the ending,nostalgic that I will miss the Sinners... but then knowing I will see them again real soon...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428127i/856390.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>For more reviews check our blog!<br><a href="http://readmore-sleepless.blogspot.gr/" rel="nofollow noopener">read more sleep less</a><br></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer485782154" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2887876458747964073"><b>5 completely magnificent stars!!!</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/547a4d8b-0c56-417b-a251-59b4d88a6651_zps1c37b8d4.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402085i/781321.jpg' alt=' photo 547a4d8b-0c56-417b-a251-59b4d88a6651_zps1c37b8d4.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>OMG this book was just amazing! The Original Sinners Series just gets better and better with each book!<br/><br/>The Prince left us with a ginormous cliffhanger... luckily, The Mistress starts off right where The Prince left off. Nora has been kidnapped. We aren’t sure what the kidnapper wants, or who... but it’s pretty clear that everything is just a game to them- <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/16c813c7-a5d3-4eaf-b6ca-d6b7be574e56_zps9728ad9e.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402085i/781322.jpg' alt=' photo 16c813c7-a5d3-4eaf-b6ca-d6b7be574e56_zps9728ad9e.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>And this game has many players...<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/1dd81167-0859-4089-9cda-f2b3d3a5d619_zpsc69291c3.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402085i/781323.jpg' alt=' photo 1dd81167-0859-4089-9cda-f2b3d3a5d619_zpsc69291c3.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/eac5f1bd-8481-420f-badb-556b3a9eb65d_zps45405cf4.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402085i/781324.jpg' alt=' photo eac5f1bd-8481-420f-badb-556b3a9eb65d_zps45405cf4.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/b0656dbf-cfc3-44b1-af3c-4c98c2a1db3d_zpsbda7d545.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402085i/781325.jpg' alt=' photo b0656dbf-cfc3-44b1-af3c-4c98c2a1db3d_zpsbda7d545.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Everyone is on a quest to save Nora. What lengths will t</span>
  <span id="freeText2887876458747964073" style="display:none"><b>5 completely magnificent stars!!!</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/547a4d8b-0c56-417b-a251-59b4d88a6651_zps1c37b8d4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402085i/781321.jpg" alt=" photo 547a4d8b-0c56-417b-a251-59b4d88a6651_zps1c37b8d4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>OMG this book was just amazing! The Original Sinners Series just gets better and better with each book!<br><br>The Prince left us with a ginormous cliffhanger... luckily, The Mistress starts off right where The Prince left off. Nora has been kidnapped. We aren’t sure what the kidnapper wants, or who... but it’s pretty clear that everything is just a game to them- <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/16c813c7-a5d3-4eaf-b6ca-d6b7be574e56_zps9728ad9e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402085i/781322.jpg" alt=" photo 16c813c7-a5d3-4eaf-b6ca-d6b7be574e56_zps9728ad9e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And this game has many players...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/1dd81167-0859-4089-9cda-f2b3d3a5d619_zpsc69291c3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402085i/781323.jpg" alt=" photo 1dd81167-0859-4089-9cda-f2b3d3a5d619_zpsc69291c3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/eac5f1bd-8481-420f-badb-556b3a9eb65d_zps45405cf4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402085i/781324.jpg" alt=" photo eac5f1bd-8481-420f-badb-556b3a9eb65d_zps45405cf4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/b0656dbf-cfc3-44b1-af3c-4c98c2a1db3d_zpsbda7d545.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402085i/781325.jpg" alt=" photo b0656dbf-cfc3-44b1-af3c-4c98c2a1db3d_zpsbda7d545.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Everyone is on a quest to save Nora. What lengths will they be willing to go? I absolutely loved how even though Nora is kidnapped and in a terrible situation, she never loses who she is or her crazy sense of humor. She is still my favorite heroine of all time! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/26d98018-0342-4945-bdf4-12f4bc363949_zps5f58b5d8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402085i/781326.jpg" alt=" photo 26d98018-0342-4945-bdf4-12f4bc363949_zps5f58b5d8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Everyone knows where Nora is, but there isn’t much they can do to get her out with out sacrificing someone else. The person that has her is seriously sick. She wants vengeance for what happened to her long ago. She doesn't care who dies... she just wants someone to...<br><b>
  <blockquote>Søren couldn’t live in a world without Nora. Kingsley couldn’t live in a world without Søren. Her death would be like the sinking of a great ship. She would take them all down with her.</blockquote>
</b><br>I loved the multiple p.o.v’s through the story- just great! We got to see a little inside everyones head- no Søren, but for some reason, he was very open with Grace so we got to see inside his head a lot through Grace’s pov. <br><br>If you had any doubts at all about how much Søren loves Nora, this book will wipe all your doubts away. <br><b>
  <blockquote>"There is nothing I wouldn't do to protect you, Eleanor. Nothing I wouldn't do to help you. And nothing I wouldn't do to save you. Nothing."</blockquote>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/83d102e2-0546-4a50-9856-33426829a50a_zps998d3a8e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402085i/781327.jpg" alt=" photo 83d102e2-0546-4a50-9856-33426829a50a_zps998d3a8e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I was always a little conflicted about their relationship, especially in the first book- now I am 100% team Søren. He is the only one for Nora in my opinion! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/23788a5a-ca96-483e-9ad9-2c7301c34b9f_zps42c2d3bd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402086i/781328.jpg" alt=" photo 23788a5a-ca96-483e-9ad9-2c7301c34b9f_zps42c2d3bd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Not everything gets tied up in a nice little bow at the end of this book, that is not this author’s style. But- a lot of things were resolved and ultimately, I am happy with most of it. I especially loved the 1:1 with Wes and Søren, then Wes and Kingsley... <br><i>
  <blockquote>“I want her to be safe.”<br> “You don’t want her to be safe. She is safe with us. You want her to be saved. You can’t save someone-” <br>“I know. I know... I can’t save someone who doesn’t want to be saved.”<br> “No. You can’t save someone who doesn’t need to be saved.”</blockquote>
</i><br>The ending... I’m not 100% sure how I feel about it. I was a little shocked, thats for sure. I wanted more- I need some of the characters reactions to that bomb that was just dropped! I was excited that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[It set up for Wes and Laila to be together. I loved Wes, but he never belonged with Nora. They are best friends, they love each other, but they just didn’t fit. I was also happy with Kingsley becoming a daddy ;D  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br>In <i>The Siren</i>, I fell in love with <b>Nora</b>. In <i>The Angel</i>, <b>Griffin </b>stole my heart. <i>The Prince</i>, I developed a soft spot for <b>Kingsley</b>... now after reading <i>The Mistress</i>, I love me some <b>Søren</b>! I’m just amazed by Tiffany’s writing- it sucks you in. Beautiful, brilliant, fantastic! Just not enough good things to say about this book! If you haven’t read this series, you are really missing out on some thing great. I can’t wait for the next installment- The Priest! More Søren... CAN’T WAIT!!!!!<br><br><b>‘Love is giving yourself to someone else. Giving yourself to someone else without losing yourself.’</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/a94d85e4-4639-48f5-ab76-98dd52ff122a_zps7d24ec4d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402086i/781329.jpg" alt=" photo a94d85e4-4639-48f5-ab76-98dd52ff122a_zps7d24ec4d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><u>SOREN &amp; NORA</u><br><b>‘I promised you forever.’<br>‘Forever isn’t long enough.’</b><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Love versus love, King. you’re comparing infinities. There is no ‘more,’ That’s not how love works. If it’s love, it’s infinite. You can’t count it.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><i>** ARC provided by Harlequin Publishing, via Netgalley in an exchange for an honest review.**</i><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_699802266" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/699802266" />
    <a title="Mo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11856352-mo"><img alt="Mo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1371247812p2/11856352.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/699802266?book_show_action=true">Aug 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mo" href="/user/show/11856352-mo">Mo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18270788-the-mistress">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer699802266" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11865450580767386094">I said not 5 stars - no, not even 55 stars ... how about 5 million stars.<br/><br/>OK, here we go…. Seriously if I had not been writing my review as I read you would be getting nothing from me tonight, or even tomorrow, NADA, NIETS … OK, Mo, you did that already. This author has blown my mind. I love her. I am speechless after reading this. The only addition I added was my trip down memory lane of the poem I learned in school, in a 4 teacher national school in the West of Ireland many moons ago…. Oh, the </span>
  <span id="freeText11865450580767386094" style="display:none">I said not 5 stars - no, not even 55 stars ... how about 5 million stars.<br><br>OK, here we go…. Seriously if I had not been writing my review as I read you would be getting nothing from me tonight, or even tomorrow, NADA, NIETS … OK, Mo, you did that already. This author has blown my mind. I love her. I am speechless after reading this. The only addition I added was my trip down memory lane of the poem I learned in school, in a 4 teacher national school in the West of Ireland many moons ago…. Oh, the innocence, the purity, the ignorance. Tiffany Reisz, you are a genius. I have some favourite authors but as of now, you are numero uno. Seriously, this series is brilliant. I see, I just said “seriously” twice in this paragraph …. Shows how much my brain cells are shot to pieces. Just “Shut the fuck up Mo and give your fucking review.” – as Nora might say.<br><br><b>“So, I’ve been meaning to ask you …”<br>“Are you one of those priests who fucks the kids in the congregation.”</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433770i/873188._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>“Because there is nothing I wouldn’t do to protect you, Eleanor. Nothing I wouldn’t do to help you. And nothing I wouldn’t do to save you. Nothing.”<br><br>Well, it has started with a BANG!! I think it is going to be good. This author, I don’t think, can write a bad book….. <br><br><br><br>LET THE GAME BEGIN …<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380823108i/3125618._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Glad to see characters from the previous books appearing… Griffin, Yum!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380823108i/3125619._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kingsley, YES!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380823108i/3125620._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Wes … don’t really give a damn.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380823108i/3125621.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>… and the man himself…<br><br><b>“Is he handsome?"<br>“Is the pope Catholic?”</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379797101i/627233._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>… and the infamous Ms. Sutherlin<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418108i/827646._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>… and Grace and Zach! They are all coming out of the woodwork.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380823108i/3125622.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Laila …<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380823108i/3125623.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and of course…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380823108i/3125624._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>" ….I gave him my death as a gift. And now I’m taking my gift back."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433770i/873189._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Only last year Kingsley had read a story in the news about a Catholic priest who’d fallen in love with a woman and married her. The consequence? Excommunication. Strange justice. Priests who molested children were put into counseling. The priests who fell in love with adults were damned. And SØREN wondered why Kingsley had never converted.</b><br><br>Seriously, this author has me thinking all over again about the Catholic Faith…. It is totally outdated. It really needs to rethink its RULES on “celibacy”. I doubt they will EVER give into women clergy…. Not in my lifetime anyway.<br><br><b>He smelled cool, clean like a new fallen snow on a winter’s night.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433770ra/873190.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380823108i/3125625._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380823108i/3125626.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Gotta love Kingsley ….<br><br><b>"What? Are you the French James Bond or something?<br>“Of course not. James Bond is vanilla."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433770i/873191._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Once upon a time …. I was fucking my friend, Griffin, when the phone rang."</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433770i/873192.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"If I choose you, Little One … I can own you. You would be my property, mine alone."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433770i/873193._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>SACRIFICE ….<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380823108i/3125627._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>"I watched you watch it …. I watched him run his fingers through your hair … I watched you."</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433770ra/873194.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh, Ms Reisz, you are good, very good indeed.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380823108i/3125628.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>"IS IT WEIRD HAVING A PRIEST FOR AN UNCLE?"</b><br><br>Try having three priests for uncles … and trust me, none of them looked like HIM! And did I mention that four of my aunts were Nuns. It’s a wonder I didn’t take the vow myself and enter an enclosed order….. think it was the fact that I saw <i>The Sound of Music</i> when I was about 14 and fell in love with Captain von Trapp and thought to myself, "Well if the cloistered life is not for Maria, then it is definitely not for me." Simple as that!<br><br><b><i>"Sláinte mhaith"</i> SØREN said, his pronounciation of the Celtic words so perfect even her Irish mother would have been impressed.</b><br><br>OMFG, he just spoke in Irish to Grace – Give me this MAN right fucking NOW. I love him.<br><br><br><b>"I’ve already had five glasses tonight."</b><br><br><b>"Five? …. I’d be underneath a table in a coma after five glasses of Merlot"</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433770i/873195.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>YEAH, me too – Jesus, five glasses of wine – dreadful!<br><br><br><b>"There’s no shame in being afraid. Even Christ was afraid in the Garden of Gethsemene. He prayed that the cup of his cruxifixion would be taken from him. And he was so scared he sweat blood …."</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433770i/873196._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380823108i/3125629.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I swear this author has me wanting go to College and study Theology….<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380823108i/3125630._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Brilliant, fucking brilliant… because when she did that, I shouted “NO!” One of the kids came downstairs to see was I alright.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380823108i/3125631.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I don’t often shed a tear reading a book but when Nora was talking about the later years … about the future.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380823108ra/3125632.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I am speechless after reading this book. Must admit I had a LOL moment at the Christopher Plummer reference. Great Minds, eh, Tiffany?<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Garce and HIM, no way, that was a total NO GO AREA for me. Not sure why she included it - probably because we are going to have the IMMACULATE CONCEPTION 9 months later. That was my only gripe with the book. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>"THE BALLAD OF FATHER GILLIGAN<br>William Butler Yeats.<br><br><blockquote>The old priest Peter Gilligan<br>Was weary night and day;<br>For half his flock were in their beds,<br>Or under green sods lay.<br><br>Once, while he nodded on a chair,<br>At the moth-hour of eve,<br>Another poor man sent for him,<br>And he began to grieve.<br><br>'I have no rest, nor joy, nor peace,<br>For people die and die';<br>And after cried he, 'God forgive!<br>My body spake, not I!'<br><br>He knelt, and leaning on the chair<br>He prayed and fell asleep;<br>And the moth-hour went from the fields,<br>And stars began to peep.<br><br>They slowly into millions grew,<br>And leaves shook in the wind;<br>And God covered the world with shade,<br>And whispered to mankind.<br><br>Upon the time of sparrow-chirp<br>When the moths came once more.<br>The old priest Peter Gilligan<br>Stood upright on the floor.<br><br>'Mavrone, mavrone! the man has died<br>While I slept on the chair';<br>He roused his horse out of its sleep,<br>And rode with little care.<br><br>He rode now as he never rode,<br>By rocky lane and fen;<br>The sick man's wife opened the door:<br>'Father! you come again!'<br><br>'And is the poor man dead?' he cried.<br>'He died an hour ago.'<br>The old priest Peter Gilligan<br>In grief swayed to and fro.<br><br>'When you were gone, he turned and died<br>As merry as a bird.'<br>The old priest Peter Gilligan<br>He knelt him at that word.<br><br>'He Who hath made the night of stars<br>For souls who tire and bleed,<br>Sent one of His great angels down<br>To help me in my need.<br><br>'He Who is wrapped in purple robes,<br>With planets in His care,<br>Had pity on the least of things<br>Asleep upon a chair.'"</blockquote></b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433770ra/873197.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_681262274" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/681262274" />
    <a title="Dinjolina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4438768-dinjolina"><img alt="Dinjolina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1538566173p2/4438768.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/681262274?book_show_action=true">Jul 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dinjolina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dinjolina" href="/user/show/4438768-dinjolina">Dinjolina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4438768-dinjolina?shelf=15-tissues-later">15-tissues-later</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4438768-dinjolina?shelf=bad-boy-involved">bad-boy-involved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4438768-dinjolina?shelf=evil-women-give-me-headaches">evil-women-give-me-headaches</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4438768-dinjolina?shelf=hero-i-wanted-dead">hero-i-wanted-dead</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4438768-dinjolina?shelf=secret-baby-pssssttt">secret-baby-pssssttt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4438768-dinjolina?shelf=2nd-chance-at-love">2nd-chance-at-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4438768-dinjolina?shelf=don-t-know-how-to-rate">don-t-know-how-to-rate</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4438768-dinjolina?shelf=hero-in-need-of-spermicide">hero-in-need-of-spermicide</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4438768-dinjolina?shelf=horribly-wrong-ending">horribly-wrong-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4438768-dinjolina?shelf=superb-heroine">superb-heroine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer681262274" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13677056985658658265"><b>I threw up.</b><br/><i>I finished ‘The mistress’ and I – <b>threw up.</b></i><br/>Not metaphorically. Not a tiny bit. I literally lost my whole lunch.<br/>Maybe it was food poisoning. Maybe it was just a weird day and I was tired. <br/>Maybe, could be, why not…<br/>…but deep in my heart – I know it was the stress.<br/><u>The wrongness.</u><br/>The tight feeling that followed me trough the whole book escalated and brought me down.<br/><i>
  <b>There was no tears. Just raw pain. So I find it fitting, and almost poetic when you consider what the basis of the Sinner se</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText13677056985658658265" style="display:none"><b>I threw up.</b><br /><i>I finished ‘The mistress’ and I – <b>threw up.</b></i><br />Not metaphorically. Not a tiny bit. I literally lost my whole lunch.<br />Maybe it was food poisoning. Maybe it was just a weird day and I was tired. <br />Maybe, could be, why not…<br />…but deep in my heart – I know it was the stress.<br /><u>The wrongness.</u><br />The tight feeling that followed me trough the whole book escalated and brought me down.<br /><i>
  <b>There was no tears. Just raw pain. So I find it fitting, and almost poetic when you consider what the basis of the Sinner series was.</b>
</i><br /><br /><i>
  <b>Have you ever eaten anything boiled in or covered with squid ink?</b>
</i><br />It has a pretty taste, but it’s <b>messy</b>, its <b>dark</b>, it’s <b>like your eating something that crawled half dead from hell</b>.<br /><i>
  <b>It’s just faulty!</b>
</i><br /><u>That’s how I felt after this book.</u> I munched, I chewed, I tried….i did. One crumb at a time. <b>
  <i>But in the end – it just wasn’t in me to except any of it.</i>
</b><br /><br /><u>Don’t get me wrong. This author is a master.</u><br />She has a way with words, and she has magic woven in to her writing. I respect all of her work, and I applaud her creativity.<br /><b>I just abhor her decisions and direction.</b><br /><br />The Sinners have come full circle.<br />I have come full circle with them.<br />On this journey I have learned something: I don’t like violence. I don’t like subterfuge. I don’t really dig any unusual things. I don’t like a lot, but I am ultimately tolerant, and I can live it down. <i>The only things that <u>can break me</u> are – broken promises, shattered hearts and raw earthy emotions.</i><br /><b>And ‘The Mistress’ broke me oh so well. It did me in.</b><br /><br />I don’t know where to start.<br />I was never completely ok with Nora’s promiscuous lifestyle.<br />I know people said that because of it she was underdeveloped and lacking, but <b>
  <i>I just thought that she is the one that gets hurt the most, because deep down – she has wants and dreams, and she understands more then others give her credit for. </i>
</b><br />Her obsession with sex is a product of her upbringing, the life she lead, and the situations she was in. I don’t think it was in her at the beginning. I don’t think she was born this way (unlike some of the other charcaters), and I don’t think it was her ultimate destiny to be become what she was. I think she was made. And that makes her more open to being wounded.<br /><br /><u>I feel like even thou so many people fall in love with her spark, they never really see her.</u><br /><br /><b>Time and time again I have found Nora left behind.</b> And not just in the obvious situations of King and Sǿren / Grace and Zach / Griffin and Michael. But in the small bits, during the tiny peaces, behind the main scenes. <b>She is constantly alone.</b> Yes, she has these big loves, but in the end – they are always moved by some other people, always influenced by some greater good or bad, some Endgame that is yet to come.<br />I remember her need to help others (even if her misguided ways are always too sexual) and I think to myself – everybody is always talking about how Sǿren is the ultimate good, that balances out even his bad side. <b>I personally think that Sǿren’s biggest good if – finding Nora. Making Nora. She is the light in the dark, and she is the brains of the operation. All of the others, even Sǿren with his philosophy, and Kingsly with his army – are ultimately just pawns.</b><br /><br /><i>Alas, there was <u>a LOT</u> of pawns in this novel.</i> And they all had their chapters and points of view. <b>It was overcrowded</b>, and I was annoyed with the constant appearances of characters that I had no connection to, while people I truly liked/loved were mysteriously absent.<br />Plus, these ‘new’ characters weren’t even bringing anything to the story. Their ‘insight’ was either boring or insignificant. They were there in order to serve as gimmicks of plot flow.<br /><b>They are also something that would be tolerated and even normal in the writing of a rookie author, but after 4 full length books and 6 companion novels, <u>I expected more.</u></b><br /><br />I have no idea what Grace was doing in this book. I never liked the idea of her, and I never understood why Zach got back with her. <i>She was a limp dishrag, and she is one still.</i> She debutes as an ultimately lame character, latching on to Nora so she could get some glitter on her skin, a spec of Nora’s brilliance.<br /><b>She was just this headless chicken, running from scene to scene, and in the end – she was rewarded for it.<i>Yes, rewarded.</i> And I don’t get why.</b><br />When the final chapter went down, I found myself betrayed <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ by <u>both Grace and Sǿren.</u><br /><b>I felt sick over the fact that he slept with her. I was racked with shivers once I realized he broke his ultimate vow of love</b> –that he would never sleep with anybody but King and Nora- <b>and for who? For what purpose? To appraise that sorry excuse of a woman?</b><br /><br />Was he attracted to her? Did he see something in her? Wasn’t he the ultimate oracle, the person that can look in to people’s soules?<br /><b>How could he not find hers completely empty and lacking?</b><br /><br />I also have a very strong suspicion that Nora was convinced he just needed somebody to beat up. Just a regular everyday sub. Let's be realistic - she had a hard time even thinking about Sǿren’s night with Kingsly, and they never talked about it.<br /><i><b>Sharing something with Grace, makes it all...soiled.</b></i> <br /><br />I was as shocked as Nora when it turned out that Grace and Zach’s baby was indeed Sǿren’s child. I was unable to label it as a happy ending, and I <b>wanted to carve Sǿren in to tiny bits</b> when he laughed over it with Zach, on the phone, in the final scene. It destroyed the previous happy moment in which Sǿren and Nora exchanged promise rings. It was horrible and unfair in light of the fact that Nora was unable to keep King’s baby, all because of circumstances that ultimately revolved around Sǿren, and yet he was completely able to just sprout his seed in to a random somebody, without thinking about the impact this would have on the partner he claims to love more than life.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />The whole surprise was lacking as well as disappointing. It almost made me analyze if the Sinners book were all a big a lie. It made me doubt the love, the affection, everything. <br /><br />Of course, the situation with Wes did not help. His new found <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[love <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> seemed to be stuck on fast-forward, and without a proper build up. When this kind of thing happened in the previous books, it was done almost acceptably, and you were just left to face the music. Alas, in “The Mistress”, the nefarious niece was one horrible plot device that was just supposed to remove an obstacle in <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the love triangle, <i>duh!</i> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />It was poorly executed, and even thou I generally was not ok with the in-your-face sexuality of some scenes featured in the Sinner books, the naïveté and the virginallity of this subplot was highly inappropriate. <b>The blatant sweetness of it was so over the top, it made your teeth ache, and the only thing your mind was able to scream was – <u>fake, fake, FAKE!</u></b><br />In other words – I could find no part of Wes, in this (new?) character. His innocence was replaced by faithlessness and he seemed almost cruel. The way he acted was compleately out of the orbit in which he normally resided. The Wes I knew and loved would have never <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[just throw Nora way after having a tiny glimpse of her and Sǿrens life, he would never not fight for her, and he would most certainly never have sex with another girl while Nora was 2 feet way. No. Not him. Not the person that believed so much in the meaningless of how we treat people and relationships. Not the man that never touched the girlfriend he was in a relationship with – because he loved Nora. No. Just No.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> So, what the author made him do - <b>completely <i>dischanted the magic that was Wes.</i></b> It made him seem erratic and juvenile, and ultimately - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <b>a flighty partner that was unfaithful to his own supposed emotions.</b>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />So, in the end, somehow, <b>
  <u>this particular book made me disillusioned about love.</u>
</b> There was always a lot going on in these series, but the focus was constantly on the strong bonds of a relationship (what ever that relationship may be) Sure, there was the sadism, the pseudo-cheating, the jealousy, but I understood it. <i>
  <b>Nobody did things just for the sake of it. Nobody was <u>fickle.</u></b>
</i><br /><br /><u>
  <b>Until now.</b>
</u><br /><br />The strongest characters fell under…<i>temptation?</i> Not even that.<br />They fell in the name of subplots, page time, and page fillers.<br />Love was shattered under to feet of newly introduced individuals that I had no connection with. Vows were broken, tears were shed, hearts were stepped on, for no reason at all. Characters lost themselves and my ultimate favorites - Sǿren and Wes – seemed to be kidnapped by aliens and replaced by bad clones.<br />A good series was ended with a bad book.<br /><u>And for what? Why? What was the point?</u><br /><i>Sadness.</i> That’s all I can feel now.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13677056985658658265" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Eda**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6285155-eda"><img alt="Eda**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581410351p2/6285155.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1141791034?book_show_action=true">Dec 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eda**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eda**" href="/user/show/6285155-eda">Eda**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6285155-eda?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1141791034" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18154232876510078255"><br/><b>
  <i>** 5 +++ "<u>checkmate</u>" STARS**</i>
</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Don't be afraid," he whispered against her lips. "This life is nothing but one blink of God's eyes. He'll blink again, and we'll be back together."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419640504ra/13105117.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>I've been avoiding this moment for the last 3 days.</i> <b>Why?</b> Because I still get teary-eyed every time I start thinking about this series. Because I am still haunted by the story, the characters, the message of love in these books. Because I am still a mess over how everything turned out at the end. <i>Happy, but </i></span>
  <span id="freeText18154232876510078255" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>** 5 +++ "<u>checkmate</u>" STARS**</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Don't be afraid," he whispered against her lips. "This life is nothing but one blink of God's eyes. He'll blink again, and we'll be back together."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419640504ra/13105117.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>I've been avoiding this moment for the last 3 days.</i> <b>Why?</b> Because I still get teary-eyed every time I start thinking about this series. Because I am still haunted by the story, the characters, the message of love in these books. Because I am still a mess over how everything turned out at the end. <i>Happy, but still hopelessly ruined.</i><br><br>I can almost hear you guys saying <i>“Dude… This is an erotica. A very explicit and unconventional one. What gives?”</i> <b>*sigh* It’s very hard to explain, really.</b> There are these books that you read and they just touch some deep spot inside your soul, changing your view of life and love, making you a different person. <b>THIS IS ONE OF THOSE BOOKS.</b> I know it's weird to get emotional over a book that consists of lots of sex, but this story is so much more than that, <i>trust me.</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387312687ra/7575047.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've praised <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4480131.Tiffany_Reisz" title="Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">Tiffany Reisz</a> enough already in my reviews for the previous books in the series, but I can't help it! It's unbelievable how f*cking brilliant this woman's writing is. You just get on this crazy roller-coaster of a story, buckle up, and let the words take you away to forbidden places. <i>It's almost as if this brilliant woman puts you in front of a mirror, forces you to reflect on who you are, what you believe, where your life is going and all you can do is say <b>“Yes, Mistress Reisz.”</b>.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419890078i/13144755._SX540_.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The presentation of the story as a <b>chess play</b> was unexpected but very much appreciated. If you are a chess player yourself and know the pieces and moves, it helps you immensely to understand the purpose of and meaning after some of the events that may fail to make sense at first glance. If you're not familiar with the game, then I suggest you make a 'lil Google search before starting to read it ;)<br><br>As for the story itself...<i>I'm not going to spill anything.</i> It needs to be experienced first hand, so I'm going to allow you the chance to do exactly that: <i>
  <b>Experience.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405485838ra/10404667.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The Queen / ♕ / Nora:</b> For once, I actually admired this wildcard's every word and action. She was absolutely fearless and never lost her faith, her integrity. Thank God she made all the right choices this time.<br><br><b>The Bishop / ♗ / Søren:</b> There are no words to properly explain the perfection of this man. If anyone still had doubts about the purity of his heart, I'm sure it would all go away after this book. He is one of those characters that will never leave me, even if 10 years pass. <i>I will always remember him whenever I smell pine on a cold winter day...</i><br><br><b>The King / ♔ / Kingsley:</b> Mon roi. My King. My poor, tortured soul. The biggest reason for my over-the-top obsession with this series. He has everything he ever wanted now and I am on cloud nine for him! My search around the world for the King of Kink, the King of the Underground, the King of the 8th Circle...for the sexiest Frenchman ever, <i>Kingsley Edge</i>, will never end! Mark my words you guys...<b>I WILL FIND THAT MAN EVENTUALLY!</b> ;)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419892256i/13144864._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The Knight / ♘ / Wesley:</b> This boy has been and still is the most confusing character in the series. One minute, I hate him for his immaturity and the next minute, I love him for his big and tender heart. It's not easy to be the dark duckling between all the whites, and <i>it's equally hard to be the only white duckling between the dark ducks of the 8th Circle.</i> He did the best he could and I couldn't be happier that he finally got his HEA.<br><br><b>The Pawn / ♙ / Laila:</b> I knew the purpose of her inclusion to the story way before she actually came in. I knew it at the mere mention of her name and her picture on Father Søren's desk in the church. And I am so happy about the ending for her part of the story. <i>She was a pawn but she is a Queen now.</i><br><br><b>The Rook / ♖ / Grace:</b> The only character that got on my nerves. Not even the evil bitch <b>Marie-Laure</b> pissed me off as much. Grace's every move, every word, every <i>“dreamy look”</i> made me cringe and my hands to grip my e-reader tighter to not throw it across the room. I hated that she left for home back to her husband <b>Zack</b> with an <b>ENORMOUS</b> gift from Søren. And that's the only thing I disliked about this book. <i>But I will even let that slide, because let's not kid ourselves...this book deserved no less than 5 stars! :)</i><br><br>I want so terribly to start reading <b>The White Years</b> now, but I feel like I need a break from all the <i>emotional turmoil</i> these characters dump on me. That said, I don't know how the hell I'm going to move on from this goddamn series while I've been dreaming about it for the last 3 nights. I'm in such an eternal blankness that I can't even enjoy the new books I read!<br><br>It's safe to say, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4480131.Tiffany_Reisz" title="Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">Tiffany Reisz</a> has royally ruined me for other authors. <i>GOD HELP ME...</i> :)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391504251ra/8401195.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i><b>P.S:</b> If any of you are curious about a certain <i>mysterious young French boy</i> (No, not Kingsley...but you're close.), then you may want to read this:</i><br><br><a href="http://www.tiffanyreisz.com/christmas-in-suite-37a" rel="nofollow noopener">CHRISTMAS IN SUITE 37A</a><br><br>///////////////////<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>** ♥ BuddyRead with my lovely pal Sandyღ ♥ **<br><br>Thank you so much for being supportive at any point that I got too emotional and started talking nonstop, baby! And also for understanding why it is so hard to let go of all these crazy-heads...</i>
</blockquote><br>///////////////////<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="18154232876510078255" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer2180033010440699324"><br/><br/><b>6+ stars ...</b><br/><br/><b>WHAT AN EPIC FINALE! Tiffany's brilliance knows no bounds!!! BRAVO, Ms. Reisz! BRAVO!!!</b><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=2vte4oj' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398457i/770126.jpg' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>To say that nothing else compares to this series would be a ginormous f*cking understatement!<br/><br/>The final installment of this epic saga didn't dissapoint <i>this</i> Original Sinners' fan in the slightest. Talk about writing a perfect finale! <br/><br/>I am not about to recap the whole book for you because you are either A: about to read it or B: have read it so why bother, right? I would like to say this though: </span>
  <span id="freeText2180033010440699324" style="display:none"><br><br><b>6+ stars ...</b><br><br><b>WHAT AN EPIC FINALE! Tiffany's brilliance knows no bounds!!! BRAVO, Ms. Reisz! BRAVO!!!</b><br><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2vte4oj" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398457i/770126.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>To say that nothing else compares to this series would be a ginormous f*cking understatement!<br><br>The final installment of this epic saga didn't dissapoint <i>this</i> Original Sinners' fan in the slightest. Talk about writing a perfect finale! <br><br>I am not about to recap the whole book for you because you are either A: about to read it or B: have read it so why bother, right? I would like to say this though: the fact that this book was written and presented to us as one wicked chess game was damn brilliant, to say the least! Certain characters took center stage in this book which, once again, was brilliantly done and done for a reason. If you happened to miss that reason then ... your loss, I guess. I thought another nice touch was how big part of the story was told via flashbacks (Nora's stories). Even though some of those things we did learn about in the past, it was nice/helpful to hear them from a different POV.<br><br>What else ... ah, yes ... Wes. He did get a chance to redeem himself (in my eyes) because, quite frankly, the kid annoyed me to death in The Prince. I guess it all worked out in the end and the boy is right where he belongs. Finally.<br><br>All in all, <i>
  <b>I</b>
</i> am happy with the outcome of this series and that is all that really matters! I can't wait for the prequels to start rolling in. Nora/Søren/King relationship way back when??? Yes, PLEASE!!!<br><br><br>Favorite quote:<br><br><i>“I was going to pay every penny I had to get you back .... Every penny I could beg, borrow or steal. And he…he went to pay with his life.”</i><br><br><br><br><br>*** April 22, 2012<br><br>I can not wait for this book!!! However, to quote Ella Frank's "Blind Obsession": <b>"... waiting is often the best part of a story,” ... “After all, once you know the story, it’s over.”</b> Reading this will definitely be bittersweet ... I can't wait to read the ending yet I don't want this story to end.</span>
