</blockquote><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402084ra/781303.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i><b>Tiffany Reisz has done it again!</b></i><br><br><i>She has created another emotional, mindblowing roller coaster ride that will leave you reeling with the after shocks long after you're finished...</i><br><br>I don't think I've ever been as conflicted about one of her stories as I was with this one. Weel, to be honest, it was mostly the last 10% of the story that left me a little confused and conflicted. Other than that, I pretty much enjoyed <i>The Mistress</i> just as much as the rest of the magnificent <i>Original Sinners</i> series!<br><br><b><i>The Mistress</i></b> picks up right were <i>The Prince</i> left off, the moment were Nora was bound and taken captive by an old and unexpected enemy from Søren and Kingsley's past. This leaves not only her fiance Wesley, but also Søren and Kingsley in distress, neither of them wants to think about what would happen if something bad were to happen to Nora...<br><br></p><blockquote>
  <b>"Søren couldn't live in a world without Nora. Kingsley couldn't live in a world without Søren. Her death would be like the sinking of a great ship. She would take them all down with her."</b>
</blockquote><br>But Nora is a tough lady, that we already knew from her various experiences in the kinky world...<br><br>The person who holds Nora captive has been observing Nora and her beloved ones for a long time and she know exactly how to play them. She knows that by destroying one player, the rest of them would be destroyed as well.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"You're like a fabric all woven together. I want to pull one thread and see you all unravel. To kill one of you will kill you all. I want to watch this happen. I want to see it unfold before my eyes."</b>
</blockquote><br><br><i>And so the game of chess begins...</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402084i/781304.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>The Queen</i> - <b>Nora.</b><br><i>The King</i> - <b>Kingsley.</b><br><i>The Prince</i> - <b>Wesley.</b><br><i>The Pawn</i> - <b>Laila.</b><br><i>The Rook</i> - <b>Grace.</b><br><i>The Priest</i> - <b>Søren.</b><br>And of course <i>The Bitch</i> herself - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <b>Marie-Laure</b>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br>While Nora is being held captive, all the others are worried and trying to come up with a solution to get her free. But getting her free might be easier said than done. Because <i>The Bitch</i>, that's what I'm calling her from now on, knows how to play games, and she knows it well. In order for Nora to stay alive, she is forced to become a <b>
  <i>Sheherazade</i>
</b>, a story teller. She is forced to tell stories of her past encounters with all of the important men in her life: Wesley, Kingsley and of course Søren.<br><br>That way we also learn a few new things about how Nora and Søren's relationship started out, and how it was immediately obvious from the start that although Nora wanted nothing more than to belong to Søren, she also had a wild and slightly dominant side, even as a young girl.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"You're trying to put a collar on a tiger. It won't turn it into a housecat."</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402084i/781305._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>***********************MINI-RANT************************<br><br>I think all the major players had an equally important value in the story, except for Grace... I just honestly didn't really see the value of her having such a big part in the story and most of the chapters written from her point of view seemed a bit redundant to me. And what I <b>
  <i>definitley</i>
</b> didn't get was <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the fact that she seemed so obsessed with Søren. I mean I get he's a highly intriguing man and that you wasn't to get to know him better. Hell, I even understand having a crush on him. I mean, who wouldn't, right!? But then, the fact that she would practically force herself on him and tell him she would sell her soul to be with him for one night, all the while being MARRIED to Zach, supposedly the love of her life...AND right before Spren was about to give his life for Nora, the love of <i>his</i> life! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> It just didn't make much sense... And then what shocked me <b>even more</b> was <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ that, after Nora was finally saved, Soren and Grace actually did spend the night together the first chance they got. And since Søren has only really slept with 3 people in his entire life, two of which that are <i>still</i> in his life, it just seemed really *really* weird and contradictory for him to suddenly have sex with Grace. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <b>BUT</b> the <b>ultimate shock</b> came right at the end when it turned out that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Soren is supposedly the father of Grace and Zach's baby... <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I mean, seriously!? <br><br><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402084ra/781306.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*********************MINI-RANT OVER*********************<br><br>What I am happy about though, is that almost all of the other players finally got their happy ending, I think <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Wesley especially deserved one and he and Laile seem perect for each other. I think she'll be a much better fit for him than Nora ;-) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I'm really glad with how everything turned out except for <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[that Grace and Søren situation ;-P <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, and I would have loved to find out everyone's reaction to the little bomb that was dropped right at the ending...<br><br>Overall, I still really enjoyed <i>The Mistress</i> and Tiffany Reisz has once again proven why <b><i>The Original Sinners</i></b>-series is one of my <b>all time favorite series</b>. Already *very much* looking forward to more <s>Soren</s> of Tiffany Reisz' talented writing in the next installment, <i>The Priest</i>.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402084i/781307._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></p><blockquote>
  <b>"Love versus love. King, you're comparing infinities. There is no 'more'. That's not how love works. If it's love, it's infinite." ♥♥</b>

<div id="review_523785798" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/523785798" />
    <a title="Karla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3024056-karla"><img alt="Karla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1324910771p2/3024056.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/523785798?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karla" href="/user/show/3024056-karla">Karla</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=intense">intense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=snarky-heroine">snarky-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=scorching-hot">scorching-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=wonderful-secondary-characters">wonderful-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=erotic">erotic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=sea-world-misting-fan-worthy">sea-world-misting-fan-worthy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=strong-willed-heroine">strong-willed-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=lots-o-crazy">lots-o-crazy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer523785798" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14750389354682301193"><br/><b>4.5 Stars!! Another masterpiece by Tiffany Reisz!! All is as is it should be in the Original Sinners world!</b><br/><br/>I didn’t think I could love these character’s any more than I already I did…I was <b>wrong!</b> I love them even more after reading <i>The Mistress</i>, <b>especially Soren!!</b> I don’t just love him, I lust him, adore him, dream about him, worship him…<b>I WANT him for my own!! </b><br/><br/>I also thought I knew all there was to know about these characters after reading the first 3 books in the series, plus novellas and shor</span>
  <span id="freeText14750389354682301193" style="display:none"><br><b>4.5 Stars!! Another masterpiece by Tiffany Reisz!! All is as is it should be in the Original Sinners world!</b><br><br>I didn’t think I could love these character’s any more than I already I did…I was <b>wrong!</b> I love them even more after reading <i>The Mistress</i>, <b>especially Soren!!</b> I don’t just love him, I lust him, adore him, dream about him, worship him…<b>I WANT him for my own!! </b><br><br>I also thought I knew all there was to know about these characters after reading the first 3 books in the series, plus novellas and short stories…<b>wrong again!</b> I had much to learn. These characters have so many layers, and as they’re peeled back and you journey along with them, through the past and the present, they literally bleed emotion. The author allows the reader to experience and feel everything along with them; it’s overwhelming and exhausting, yet utterly satisfying. I can’t get enough of them… especially Soren! I wanted to crawl inside the book, lay down on top of him, next to him, under him and wrap my love around him. Absorb all of him; because no one loves like he does, with everything he is, his heart and soul, he gives himself over completely! Soren is such a contradiction. He has the patience of a saint, and inflicts brutality like the devil! <br><br>There is a conversation in the book where Wesley confronts Soren, he goes in balls to the wall, guns a blazin’…he wants answers! Soren, only as Soren can, lays it all out there for him. It was my favorite scene in the book and if you didn’t love Soren by this point, you couldn’t help but fall in love with him, especially after hearing what he has to say to Wesley. <br><br><b>
  <i>“How are you like this?” he demanded, the questions pour- ing out of him like wine into a glass. “How are you a priest and a sadist? How can you say you love God and yet you sleep with Nora? How can you hit women and still claim to be a man of the cloth? How are you…you? I can’t figure you out, not to save my life.”</i>
</b><br><br>Soren never undermines Wesley’s love for Nora, he just explains how they, Nora and Soren, came to be, and with that you feel the enormity of the love he has for her. It was truly beautiful and very telling. <br><br>Kingsley is Kingsley, overbearing, protective, slinging his trademark sarcasm…his usual kinky loveable self! He’s had my heart for a long time, and his journey finally comes full circle and with it sadness, but also a tremendous amount of joy. I feel that he finally found some peace, and nothing could have made me happier.<br><br>Nora was amazing. I’ve always enjoyed her character, but there was something extra special about her in this book. When she has her blunt and frank, tell-all conversations with Marie-Laure, her tough exterior seemed to melt away and you could feel the love she has for so many people in her life. We got the softer side of this strong confident woman. <br><br>My only issue was with Grace and what played out with her, I found her to be annoying, and she didn’t add much to the story except in the end. We are shocked, maybe angry…but do we have reason to be?! Only time will tell. I would have much rather that Zach had an active role in this book. Now that would have been interesting; all the men from the series coming together to rescue the lovely Nora. <br><br>Lots of matters were resolved and I felt that everyone was in a good place by the end of the book, the right place, with the right person.<br> <br>With Tiffany Reisz nothing is cut and dry, she plays with the reader’s emotions, takes the long way around to get to the goods, and just when you think you have it figured out, the plot becomes more complex. So I say, immerse yourself in the story, savor the writing, think about what the author is saying and try to see it through the character’s eyes and emotions. Expect the unexpected, and if you can do all that, you will enjoy the journey….and my oh my, what a journey it is!! <br><br><b>GAAAAAHH!! I can’t get enough of MY SOREN!! Mine...all mine...RAWRRRR!!</b><br><a href="http://s1130.photobucket.com/user/kparks823/media/markvalley_zps45a0254f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379797439i/631781.jpg" alt=" photo markvalley_zps45a0254f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>*ARC courtesy Harlequin Mira via NetGalley*</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="14750389354682301193" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_648233263" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/648233263" />
    <a title="Jennifer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4482512-jennifer"><img alt="Jennifer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1374781588p2/4482512.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/648233263?book_show_action=true">Jun 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/4482512-jennifer">Jennifer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4482512-jennifer?shelf=lol">lol</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4482512-jennifer?shelf=tears-sniff">tears-sniff</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4482512-jennifer?shelf=rocked-my-world">rocked-my-world</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4482512-jennifer?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4482512-jennifer?shelf=mindfuck">mindfuck</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer648233263" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2397998640480696210"><b>
  <i>If it’s love, it’s infinite.</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>5 GALAXIES of STARS!!!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426371i/851973._SX540_.jpg' alt='Wedding rings on chess board' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>I thought I knew terror before today. I was wrong.</i>
</b><br/><br/>Nora is captured at the end of The Prince, so this book begins there. She is loved by many, and all those that love her are chess pieces in this rescue mission to save Nora. I had no idea how Ms. Reisz would conclude this story. To be honest, I didn’t really care. This is more than just characters and a story and a laugh and a cry. It’s just….more.<br/><br/>I’m a different person after reading this</span>
  <span id="freeText2397998640480696210" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>If it’s love, it’s infinite.</i>
</b><br><br><b>5 GALAXIES of STARS!!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426371i/851973._SX540_.jpg" alt="Wedding rings on chess board" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>I thought I knew terror before today. I was wrong.</i>
</b><br><br>Nora is captured at the end of The Prince, so this book begins there. She is loved by many, and all those that love her are chess pieces in this rescue mission to save Nora. I had no idea how Ms. Reisz would conclude this story. To be honest, I didn’t really care. This is more than just characters and a story and a laugh and a cry. It’s just….more.<br><br>I’m a different person after reading this book/series. I feel alive. This series has put a ripple in my soul. I look at myself and those that I love in a new and better way. My definition of love…has changed. I certainly view sex differently! I see God in a new way (sorry to get spiritual, but if you’ve read these books, you know it’s impossible not to). The world stopped spinning when I was reading this book.<br><br>Nora – The Queen. She is a story-teller in this book, and a lot of blanks are filled in for us because of her stories/flashbacks. She is her usual funny-as-fuck self in this book, but we get to see a more vulnerable side to Nora, while still keeping her humor. <br><br><b>
  <i>Our Nora has a magic pussy. It’s the opposite of the Bermuda Triangle. Lost men sail into it and then find themselves. </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>In my world slut is a term of endearment.</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>You know Soren’s not a vampire, right? He’s a sadist. You don’t turn kinky just because he bites you.</i>
</b><br><br>Soren – Which chess piece is he? You’ll have to read to find out. He’s always right. He is good. He is….Soren.<br><br><b>
  <i>And you come along and see him putting a knife in someone’s chest and you scream, ‘Murderer!’ while the rest of us see a heart surgeon.</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>There was no past tense with Soren. When he loved, what he loved, who he loved, he loved eternally.</i>
</b><br><br>Oh Kingsley – The King. <b>
  <i>King of Kink. King of the Underground. </i>
</b>My favorite. I want him to own me. I’d cut off my right arm to be his Juliette for a day.<br><br><b>
  <i>Are you the French James Bond or something?.....Of course not. James Bond is vanilla.</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>He speaks and your panties spontaneously combust.</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>He doesn’t want to get hurt. He wants to be destroyed.</i>
</b><br><br>Wesley – The Knight. I was not disappointed with Wesley’s fate/destiny in this book. <br><br><b>
  <i>In her heart Wesley was love and light and big brown eyes that made her thighs melt.</i>
</b><br><br>Laila – The Pawn. Laila is Soren’s niece, and this is the first time we meet her. I wasn’t sure what to think because she was such a new character, but I grew to love her very soon (because Ms. Reisz is a genius and could make me love any character that she weaves). It was interesting and fulfilling to see the role that she played in the chess game.<br><br>Grace (Zach’s Grace) – The Rook. It was wonderful to learn more about Grace. She is witty and fun and maternal, in a way. She is more important in this story than you would think. She is a wonderful surprise!<br><br><i>**Note to the author - Ms. Reisz, you are officially my #1 favorite author of all time!! I can count on one hand the authors that can make me laugh and cry at the same time, and you are one of them. An endless smile and row of tears.</i><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="2397998640480696210" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_449242929" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/449242929" />
    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/449242929?book_show_action=true">Nov 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18270788-the-mistress">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=keeper-shelf">keeper-shelf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=dark-read">dark-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=july-2013">july-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=auto-buy-authors">auto-buy-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=best-of-the-best">best-of-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-heroine">favorite-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=br">br</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=unforgettables">unforgettables</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer449242929" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2795577941040164578"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764773._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>This book! Holy shit, THIS BOOK! I must have changed my rating for it at least 5 times. After sleeping on it, I knew that even if there were things that happened that I wasn't happy about, I still couldn't rate this anything less than 5 absolutely stellar stars.<br/><br/>What are some words that I'd use to describe this series? Brilliant, Erotic, Dark and Captivating are just some of the few that come to mind.<br/><br/>The Mistress takes off right where the cliffhanger in The Prince left off, and brings us to the c</span>
  <span id="freeText2795577941040164578" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764773._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This book! Holy shit, THIS BOOK! I must have changed my rating for it at least 5 times. After sleeping on it, I knew that even if there were things that happened that I wasn't happy about, I still couldn't rate this anything less than 5 absolutely stellar stars.<br><br>What are some words that I'd use to describe this series? Brilliant, Erotic, Dark and Captivating are just some of the few that come to mind.<br><br>The Mistress takes off right where the cliffhanger in The Prince left off, and brings us to the conclusion of a series that has captivated and enthralled us from the very first page of the very first book.<br><br>I know that no review I can ever write will do the book or the absolutely fucking brilliant writing in it justice. But the best advise I can give to those about to read or even those that have read it already and are not familiar with chess, is to familiarize yourself with it. Trust me! Everything will make so much more sense. So in the hopes of clearing a few things up, since I knew a total of nilch about chess when I delved into it, I'll try to explain some things in my review.<br><br><i>The ultimate objective of the game is to capture the opponents king. </i><br><br>The book is told in several players' POV. There is The King, The Queen, The Pawn, The Rook, and The Knight.<br><br>It is also broken up into parts; Capture, En Passant, Castling, Promotion, and Checkmate.<br><br><b>The Players:</b><br><b>
  <i>The King</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379797101i/627233._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Because there is nothing I wouldn't do to protect you, Eleanor. Nothing I wouldn't do to help you. And nothing I wouldn't do to save you. Nothing."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Soren does was the one character that never got a POV in these books. In The Mistress everything we learn about Soren is garnered from his conversations with Grace and flashback stories told by Nora.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379797101i/627231._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I hate a love/hate relationship with Kingsley in the previous books. Part of it, I absolutely loved him and his humor. Parts of it I thought he came off as a whiny brat. I absolutely adored Kingsley in this book; his personality and sense of humor, and his complete and utter devotion to those he cares for. Kingsley makes it his mission to rescue Nora from the clutches of his long-presumed-dead sister. <br><blockquote>
  <b>"I get her out."<br>"You and what army?"<br>"I don't need an army."<br>"What, are you the French James Bond or something?"<br>"Of course not. James Bond is vanilla."</b>
</blockquote><br>The book gives the reader alternating POV's, with a few new players added to the mix.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764774._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>There's Wes, The Knight:</b> <br>I adored Wesley in the other 3 books, but he drove me batshit in this one. His constant refusal to understand Nora's lifestyle got old real quick. He came off as judgmental and immature little boy for most of the book. <br><br><b>Grace, The Rook:</b><br>Grace, I think for me, was the odd-one out as far as characters go. I really disliked her for most of the book, and ESPECIALLY in the end.<br>But upon further reflection, I can't even dwell on that anymore. After I googled The Rook and its moves in chess it put EVERYTHING into perspective for me. This is the absolutely FUCKING BRILLIANCE of Tiffany Reisz. There is not one wasted word, sentence, paragraph, or chapter. Everything is linked together. The character (chess piece) roles, the chess strategy names, EVERYTHING! <br><br><b>Laila, The Pawn</b><br>Laila, Soren's niece, was a new character that was introduced in this book. I had a feeling the entire time of where her role was leading, and found out I was right. I can understand the direction of this, ultimately, I felt it was a fitting conclusion.<br><br><b>Nora, The Queen</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764775._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Nora, the infamous Nora, I fucking LOVED Nora. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764776._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Marie-Laure</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764777.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I'm at a loss for words here. Simply put?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396624ra/764778.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When I finished this book, I'm pretty sure I had a day long rant about the ending (Thanks, Jamie for being my ultimate ranting buddy *waves*) Thank God I read this in a BR with the some of my fave girls, so I had some outlet for all my feels. I'm pretty sure I would have gone crazy otherwise. Oh and Amy, girl if it hadn't been for you pointing out the chess reference...I doubt I would have ever thought to do it. So thanks! ;)<br><br>Ultimately, though the ending was not the perfect HEA you would envision for a book, I though it was very fitting for this series. It was never a romance novel, so a typical romantic and perfectly wrapped up HEA would not have been accurate, fitting, or fair to these characters.<br><br>I'll be honest, I HATED it at first. But when I talked it out with my GR friends, I felt slightly better. What really sealed it for me, was understanding the Chess Strategies that broke up this book.<br><br><b>Castling</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(as described on chess.com- like I said, I was clueless in chess)<br>This move allows two important things all in one move: get your king to safety, and get the rook into the game. <br><br>Interesting to note that this was the part that Grace finally went from simply being someone that talked to Soren and was just there, to finally taking action. When Soren goes to give himself up to ML, Grace knows that she has to act in order to save him. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Promotion</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>Pawns have a special ability and that is that if a pawn reaches the other side of the board it can become any other chess piece (called promotion). A pawn may be promoted to any piece. A pawn is usually promoted to a queen. Only pawns may be promoted.<br><br>Interesting to note that in the part of the book titled Promotion, Laila gets together with Wes (the King of Kentucky), essentially becoming the Queen Of Kentucky) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Checkmate</b><br>Speaks for itself, really.<br><br>I really thought this was the perfect ending to an absolutely phenomenal series. Though left with a few questions in the end <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Kingsley's bastard son? I hate that it leaves us hanging without having this be confirmed <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I have come to accept it.<br><br>On a final note,<br>Tiffany Reisz, woman, YOU.ARE.FUCKING.BRILLIANT!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396624ra/764779.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you haven't read this series yet, what the hell are you waiting for?!!<br><br>Links to my reviews on the rest of the books in the series:<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/449242687" rel="nofollow noopener">The Siren</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/449242854" rel="nofollow noopener">The Angel</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/449242869" rel="nofollow noopener">The Prince</a><br><br><i>**ARC courtesy of publisher via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review**</i><br><br>For more reviews visit: <a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> Dirty Girl Romance Book Blog </a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_633408685" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/633408685" />
    <a title="Kim  *Mo Chridhe*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe"><img alt="Kim  *Mo Chridhe*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431962494p2/9909997.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/633408685?book_show_action=true">Jun 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kim  *Mo Chridhe*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kim  *Mo Chridhe*" href="/user/show/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe">Kim  *Mo Chridhe*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe?shelf=mind-f-ck">mind-f-ck</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe?shelf=net-galley">net-galley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe?shelf=favourite-heroines">favourite-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe?shelf=major-book-hangover">major-book-hangover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe?shelf=favourites-and-obsessions">favourites-and-obsessions</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe?shelf=books-that-made-me-cry">books-that-made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe?shelf=smutty-or-sexy-reads">smutty-or-sexy-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer633408685" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7135387534917248579"><b> - July 2 edit -</b><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424205i/845629._SY540_.jpg' width='300' height='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/>This is the review I've been dreading to write for weeks. I think writing my college thesis was less nerve-wracking. It's not because I fear tomatoes being thrown my way (look, I gave it 5 stars) but rather, I worry that I wouldn't be able to express my thoughts coherently without breaking down into a sobbing mess. <br/><br/>The Mistress picks up immediately where The Prince left off. Nora is held captive by an enemy who wants to play games. <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ And in case you're wondering</span></span>
  <span id="freeText7135387534917248579" style="display:none"><b> - July 2 edit -</b><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424205i/845629._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>This is the review I've been dreading to write for weeks. I think writing my college thesis was less nerve-wracking. It's not because I fear tomatoes being thrown my way (look, I gave it 5 stars) but rather, I worry that I wouldn't be able to express my thoughts coherently without breaking down into a sobbing mess. <br><br>The Mistress picks up immediately where The Prince left off. Nora is held captive by an enemy who wants to play games. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ And in case you're wondering who it is, well, let's just say that your hunch after reading The Prince is right.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> She is used as a pawn to lure Kingsley and Soren - the two people this kidnapper wants to hurt the most. And while Nora waits for a chance to escape or be rescued she buys time by telling tales of her relationship with the most important men in her life. <br><br>Even though the book takes place in a span of a mere few days it is not even slightly uneventful. I thought that I knew all there is to know about our beloved characters through The Prince but I was proven wrong, because this book allowed me to know them more intimately than ever. It is not just Nora who's reliving her past through her stories though. While her loved ones wait in despair, they each recall memories of Nora and share how those memories relate to themselves in the present. The narration was brilliantly done, and every few pages I'd find myself wanting to hold them close while they're bathed in worry and sadness. <br><br>It is <b>not</b> a tortuous book by all means. After all, where Nora is involved one can expect humor and sass. But there is definitely a good amount of thrill and heart-stopping moments, as there are plenty of sob-inducing ones. I CANNOT say enough how much I love Ms. Reisz's characters. Each and every person stepped up to the plate and carried out their important roles. If you think that it is impossible to love who you love even more then prepare to be schooled because every previous feeling you've felt will only be magnified here. I've never hidden the fact that I am a book crier. Nostalgia is my favourite torture device, and when I've barely made it past 1% and the waterworks have begun, then I know that the book is a winner. <br><blockquote>
  <b>"There is nothing I wouldn't do to protect you, Eleanor. Nothing I wouldn't do to help you. And nothing I wouldn't do to save you. Nothing."</b>
</blockquote><br>Lastly, I want to discuss what I felt about the ending. My initial reaction after finishing The Mistress was dumbstruck amazement. And while I sat there waiting for the one-month-before-release-date-mark so I could post my review I thought about certain events and analyzed them beyond dissection. I began to doubt my feelings for one specific part and even went as far as making up these ridiculous theories on how <b>it</b> couldn't be possibly true. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b>Theory 1:</b> <i>They</i> didn't. They engaged in breath-play and she passed out before anything could happen. <b>Theory 2:</b> <i>They</i> did, BUT, the baby isn't his. After all, only the origin of his name was revealed, and it didn't say that he actually had hair of THAT color. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> My vanilla brain couldn't accept the truth that was staring at me in the face<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[but after Ms. Reisz confirmed what I doubted at first, I felt that the balloon I was in burst <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I wallowed for a couple of days, but then I looked over the passages I highlighted and the feelings I initially felt resurfaced. I reread the entire book yesterday and now I can say with utmost conviction that everything that has happened can only be viewed as a gift. How can I possibly see a wrong in something that is so right? Have I not always mentioned in my reviews that I only want for my characters to be happy and have no regrets? And truly, there are no regrets here. I am happy for all of them and <b>I cannot wish for this book to have ended any other way.</b> My current sadness only stems from the fact that the series, chronologically, stops here. This truly is one of the best series I have ever read - best stories, best characters, best written, most captivating, most touching, most seductive, plus all the other superlatives I can't think of at the moment. Eventually, I know I'd have to move on just as my Sinners have, but for certain, this will remain a favourite for all time. <br><blockquote>
  <b>"If it's love, it's infinite."</b>
</blockquote><br><i>*This advanced copy was provided by Harlequin through Netgalley in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*&lt;*~*~*~*~*~*<br><br><br><b>Squeeeeee!!!!!! ARC request approved! Can I call in sick for the rest of the week? </b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424205ra/845630.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_649355334" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/649355334" />
    <a title="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14351108-deanna-pink-lady"><img alt="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1370640721p2/14351108.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/649355334?book_show_action=true">Jun 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" href="/user/show/14351108-deanna-pink-lady">Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer649355334" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9442121665493764887"><b> 5 "Infinite" Stars</b><br/><br/>I'm on an "Original Sinners" high at the moment and I don't want to come down for a while. There are times when you read a book or a series that affects you in a deep and emotional level and you are forever changed. To read words that evoke all your emotions, <b>good- bad-kinky-vanilla-erotic-sensual-love-sorrow-despair-fear-sadness-happiness-piety</b> you will forever remember that book or that series and folks, if you what that moment, look no further than The Original Sinners Seri</span>
  <span id="freeText9442121665493764887" style="display:none"><b> 5 "Infinite" Stars</b><br><br>I'm on an "Original Sinners" high at the moment and I don't want to come down for a while. There are times when you read a book or a series that affects you in a deep and emotional level and you are forever changed. To read words that evoke all your emotions, <b>good- bad-kinky-vanilla-erotic-sensual-love-sorrow-despair-fear-sadness-happiness-piety</b> you will forever remember that book or that series and folks, if you what that moment, look no further than The Original Sinners Series.<br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Gifs/tumblr_lvn94d7UZK1r3zat8_zps20d52c3a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424749ra/846962.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lvn94d7UZK1r3zat8_zps20d52c3a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Gifs/tumblr_inline_mifis2HnOa1qz4rgp_zpsa77f5e11.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426110ra/851064.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mifis2HnOa1qz4rgp_zpsa77f5e11.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The Mistress picks up right where The Prince left off. Nora has been kidnapped by a psychotic player from the past, someone intent on vengeance and Soren and Kingley have figured out......Marie-Laure. While being held hostage, Nora must relive stories of her past in order to gain more time. This is where the extraordinary genius of the story lies, IMO. We get the past told by Nora, her sassiness at it's finest, her feelings in the truest form. <br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/mistresscollage_zpsba96907c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426532i/852369._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo mistresscollage_zpsba96907c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Wes, Grace-Zach's wife, and Laila-Soren's niece, have all become part of the quest to rescue Nora. Each one an important chess piece in this dangerous game of chess. Each one going through a discovery....there is no way to talk about it without spoiling something. The interactions of Soren, Kingsley, Wes, Laila and Grace during Nora's absence was truly a plot of pure ecstasy.<br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/mistress2collage_zps873c52c3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426532i/852370._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo mistress2collage_zps873c52c3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I must confess that this whole series has affected me in a profound way. The writing was so raw and real and made me feel the every emotion that these characters experienced. The intertwined stories of all these people(I think of them as my friends now)and how I came to understand and not judge them was extraordinary. I really have not wanted to read anything else for fear that it will not live up to my expectations. Tiffany Reisz has spoiled me rotten, not by the subject matter, but by how exquisitely she writes.<br><br><b>"...Lose yourself inside me. Forget what you've lost, forget what you can't have. There's no shame in trying to forget for a night even if you know you'll remember in the morning."<br><br>"I'd fear she would spurn me. Instead, she said she belonged to me from the moment we met, and her body was mine to do with what I wanted. She loved me. She trusted me. She knew I wouldn't hurt her. And we kissed for the first time, and I felt something I never dreamed I'd feel."<br>"Happy?"<br>"Normal. I felt normal. I'd felt loved in the past, and I'd certainly felt happy. But never normal."<br><br>"I'll forgive because you've asked me to, not because you need my forgiveness. You did what you had to. You had to leave to become who you were meant to be. All that matters now is that you're here, Little One."<br><br>I know that love is giving yourself to someone else. Giving yourself to someone without losing yourself.<br><br>"I always loved you. I never once stopped loving you. All those times I said I hated you, I never meant them, not once. I loved every part of you, every secret, every sin. I love what you are and what you do and how you make me feel so scared and so safe all at the same time, God I wish I had my collar."</b><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Gifs/tumblr_m5wdemqFH81r0byljo1_400_zps4a000362.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424749ra/846959.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m5wdemqFH81r0byljo1_400_zps4a000362.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I could go on and one with beautiful quotes.....I loved every single part of this book and my highlighter was going all the time. It's a beautiful series and it will be in my all time favorite top 5.<br><br>BR with Jxxx. I loved that so many fabulous ladies (Mo, Irene, Shannon and Stella) helped us in the discussion and also helped me when I needed talking down from the ledge. Smooches ladies and look forward to more discussions and hopefully new BRs with ya'll too!!<br><br>Finally and proudly, I'm....<br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/angel1_zps2bd10678.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426532i/852371.jpg" alt=" photo angel1_zps2bd10678.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/mistress_zps5fc3a34c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426532i/852372.jpg" alt=" photo mistress_zps5fc3a34c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br></span>

    <a title="Saint Monique" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/40572117-saint-monique"><img alt="Saint Monique" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559130947p2/40572117.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1737440166?book_show_action=true">Jul 17, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Saint Monique" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Saint Monique" href="/user/show/40572117-saint-monique">Saint Monique</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40572117-saint-monique?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40572117-saint-monique?shelf=omg-i-am-in-love-with-this-book">omg-i-am-in-love-with-this-book</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1737440166" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13071935950529560650"><b>5 <i>'Love is infinite'</i> stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Don’t be afraid,” he whispered against her lips. “This life is nothing but one blink of God’s eyes. He’ll blink again, and we’ll be back together.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1582660492ra/29019318.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Love versus love. King, you’re comparing infinities. There is no ‘more.’ That’s not how love works. If it’s love, it’s infinite. You can’t count it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>First read: 17 Jul 2017 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br/>Re-read: 10 Mar 2020 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br/><br/><i>Warning: the usual stuff. If you've been reading my reviews for this series then you should've al</i></span>
  <span id="freeText13071935950529560650" style="display:none"><b>5 <i>'Love is infinite'</i> stars</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Don’t be afraid,” he whispered against her lips. “This life is nothing but one blink of God’s eyes. He’ll blink again, and we’ll be back together.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1582660492ra/29019318.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Love versus love. King, you’re comparing infinities. There is no ‘more.’ That’s not how love works. If it’s love, it’s infinite. You can’t count it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>First read: 17 Jul 2017 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br>Re-read: 10 Mar 2020 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br><br><i>Warning: the usual stuff. If you've been reading my reviews for this series then you should've already been aware of possible spoilers because I get carried away when Sinners are concerned, lots of mushy moments because I just can't help myself, too many quotes because it's so hard to choose and me raving about how much I adore Kingsley and Søren and all the sinners.</i><br><br>The Mistress is the last book in The Red Years Quartet and it is in a way the end of a certain storyline. Secrets are revealed, unanswered questions gets answered, debts are paid... but on the other hand, the end is only a new beginning. And that's what The White Years Quartet is all about - the new beginning. But let's not get too much ahead.<br><br>There is so much going on in The Mistress. I think it's the most unique book in the entire series. It has many POVs (five to be precise), the pace of the story is very fast and it's more like erotic romance - slash - mysterious thriller. Therefore, it's quite difficult to say anything without giving away too much and spoil the delightful surprises. That's why I'm gonna give you my review in beautiful and wonderful quotes.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b><i>Jabberwocky,</i> Nora, age eighteen, had answered on the day Søren started training her. <i>I always loved that monster.<br>He was always my favorite monster,</i> Søren had said.<br>And Nora, then still just Eleanor, remembered smiling at him, kissing him...<br><i>You’re my favorite monster</i>, she said against his lips.</b>
</blockquote><br>***********************************<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I knelt at his feet because I felt like that’s where I belonged. And no, not because I was so unworthy of him, but because he was so utterly worthy of my devotion.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I always found this quote to be powerful. It really shows how equal Søren and Nora are in their relationship. Nora owns Søren as much as he owns her. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Mon roi,” she whispered, and Kingsley’s heart clenched at the name she called him only in their most private moments. “Please, be safe. I need you.”<br>A thousand times she’d whispered that to him...breathed it across silk sheets as she crawled to him, moaned it into his ear as he entered her. But those words had a new meaning now that had nothing to do with passion anymore.<br>“I need you, too,” he said. “I need you to do as I tell you. Stay there. Stay safe. You’ll be home soon.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>One of the most tender and beautiful scenes in the book. I'm glad that despite Juliette being far away, she and Kingsley still get to share this precious moment of love. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Søren loved Kingsley...loves Kingsley,” she corrected. There was no past tense with Søren. When he loved, what he loved, who he loved, he loved eternally. “Sometimes the only way to show someone you love them is to let them go. It’s hard, though. It’s so fucking hard.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>***********************************<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“But you must know it takes nothing away from us, away from my love for you, any more than my love for you takes anything away from what I feel for him. Not that he understands that.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Heartbreakingly beautiful!! All these emotions!! Among all the love stories in this series, I always felt the most for Søren and Kingsley. Probably because they had to walk the roughest path to finally be together.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Nora regretted every last time she’d told Søren she hated him. Hopefully, he knew she never meant it, that she only said it because she didn’t know how else to tell him how annoying it was to be loved that much by someone who was so right all the damn time about everything.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>***********************************<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I always loved you. I never once stopped loving you. All those times I said I hated you, I never meant them, not once. I loved every part of you, every secret, every sin. I love what you are and what you do and how you make me feel so scared and so safe all at the same time.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>As far as love declarations go, this one is everything!!<br><br>There were so many more beautiful moments in this book. Between Griffin and Michael, between Zachary and Grace, I could say among all the characters. The whole book is like an ode to love. The love between lovers, love between friends, family love. But unless I copy the whole book in my review, there is not a single chance I can give justice to have much I loved this story. If you want a book to inspire you, that is the one.<br><br><i>B(R)R with my Sinner Ladies ❤❤❤❤❤ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/52957386-melanie-a" rel="nofollow noopener">Melanie</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/58429822-ursy" rel="nofollow noopener">Ursy</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/14379473-leila" rel="nofollow noopener">Leila</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/66575688-whitney" rel="nofollow noopener">Whitney</a>. What an awesome journey we've had so far and we are only at the half of it.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="13071935950529560650" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_740093230" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/740093230" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/740093230?book_show_action=true">Oct 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=dark-taboo-forbidden-reads">dark-taboo-forbidden-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=drop-everything-and-read-it-now">drop-everything-and-read-it-now</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=top-rated">top-rated</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=panty-dropping-hot">panty-dropping-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-love-my-friends">i-love-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=6-stars-of-brilliance">6-stars-of-brilliance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=dark-reads">dark-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=special-and-precious">special-and-precious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=10-stars-of-extraordinary">10-stars-of-extraordinary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer740093230" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6247898966099485832"><u>EDIT 12/28/13 from the Mistress herself:</u> "Also in 2014, the first four books of The Original Sinners are being released with new covers with bonus short stories at the end. You'll finally be able to own "Gauze," "Griffin in Wonderland," "Midnight Mass," and "A Beautiful Thing" in print."<br/><br/><b> 10+++++ stars!!!! This one and The Angel are my favorites in the series! Oh and EFF Fifty Shades, read this series instead!</b><br/><br/>Now that I’m done with The Red Years Quartet, I feel empty and like I lost my purpose in</span>
  <span id="freeText6247898966099485832" style="display:none"><u>EDIT 12/28/13 from the Mistress herself:</u> "Also in 2014, the first four books of The Original Sinners are being released with new covers with bonus short stories at the end. You'll finally be able to own "Gauze," "Griffin in Wonderland," "Midnight Mass," and "A Beautiful Thing" in print."<br /><br /><b> 10+++++ stars!!!! This one and The Angel are my favorites in the series! Oh and EFF Fifty Shades, read this series instead!</b><br /><br />Now that I’m done with The Red Years Quartet, I feel empty and like I lost my purpose in life...I wish I could unread this entire series and be able to read it again to live it all once more.<br /><br />I’ve had a full day to mull over just how important this series has become to me, and why the heck is it so compelling when many aspects of the book usually make me run for the hills. <br /><br /><b>First and foremost, I think the “romantic” nature of this series stood out to me.</b> For the past few hours, I’ve clashed heads with other TOS readers that argue these books should not be classified as romance. I beg to differ. In fact, I believe the “Søren/Nora/Kingsley plus a side of Wesley” complex to be the most romantic tale of all time (so MOVE OUT Shakespeare!!!) It’s <b>
  <i>certainly</i>
</b> not a conventional romance, that’s for sure, but Tiffany Reisz is no conventional writer. No, she pushes your buttons, crosses all sorts of boundaries, and does not hold back. I don’t say this to purposely romanticize the series. It’s done a magnificent job of that on its own. In The Siren, when you have Nora and Søren, the two MC that readers are <i>actually</i> rooting for to be a couple in all senses of the world but just can’t be, subtly and passionately bringing Zach and Grace together, who <i>
  <b>isn’t</b>
</i> touched by these characters’ innate romantic side? <br /><br />And in The Angel? Nora and Søren are together, but cruel fate and Søren’s religious career threatens their relationship, and they are separated once more. They do not bemoan their fate. They do not whine about the circumstances. They love each other, simple as that, and will do anything for one another. So once again, Nora and Søren are apart, yet they bring another couple together. Griffin and Michael find true love, and no matter how kinky or unorthodox their relationship, it doesn’t take away from the pure beauty and magnificence of their love. <br /><br />The Prince? IMO, the most romantic of the quartet, and presents the strongest, most passionate M/M love I have <i>
  <b>ever</b>
</i> read. Yes, Søren and Kingsley’s relationship has always been brutal as Ms. Reisz narrates Søren’s sadistic needs and Kingsley’s ‘switch’ nature, but does that take away from their individual personalities? Does it dismiss their claims of love for one another? Heck no! It only makes it THAT more <b>
  <i>real</i>
</b>, more <b>
  <i>raw</i>
</b>, and in my opinion, more romantic than ever. <br /><br />Finally, we get to The Mistress. I don’t want to reveal the specifics of what happens in this book, but just know that only Ms. Reisz could make the whole slew of characters come to a full circle and give each and every one of them the ending they <b>
  <i>deserve</i>
</b>. Not what reader opinion calls for, but what each and every one of these unique characters deserve. And I sure got a kick out of the ending! I personally think Ms. Reisz served a plate of smack-down noodles with it! You don’t expect her to write a sappy, full of mush and goo ending. There are readers out there unsatisfied by this fourth book, but for this reader? It couldn’t have been more perfect. Truly written with an edgy, intriguing signature. Reisz style. <br /><br /><b>The core value of the book deeply resonated with me</b>. Ms. Reisz skyrockets the taboo and controversial level in TOS, but that wasn’t what made me connect with these books. The fact of the matter is despite the characters having different values than what the norm expects (believing in love but not necessarily monogamy), they wouldn’t hesitate to support one another, to love each other, to sacrifice themselves for another. I’m talking about through life, death, and life again. Their inner strength, their core spirit, their resilience, is what turns these characters into <i>people</i>, and they become real in my mind. Are they flawed for having different thoughts, different romantic beliefs, different sexual fetishes that are out of the norm? HECK NO! These people embrace their beliefs and at the same time, take care to not harm others in their path. How can one <b>
  <i>not</i>
</b> admire these characters’ strength? Their passion for life? Their fearless attitude towards death? I, for one, am weeping as I write this part because <b>
  <i>never</i>
</b> have I read such emotionally compelling characters that make me FEEL and experience so much at one time. <br /><br /><b>The flawless writing style. Fluid. Conducive. Unapologetic. Romantic. <i>Simply perfect</i></b>. How does Ms. Reisz do it? How does she make each and every one of her words, no letters, into something monumental, something unforgettable? How does she do it? I don’t need to know. I don’t want to know. Please, Ms. Reisz, continue to surprise me with your ingenious writing. <br /><br />What more could this reader ask for? What more could I possibly ask for after reading this stunning, groundbreaking series? Nothing (well the next book would be nice). From one humble reader to this astounding author, I bow at your feet. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6247898966099485832" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=swoon-worthy">swoon-worthy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=stoppp-it-hurts">stoppp-it-hurts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=sequel">sequel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=hotness-alert">hotness-alert</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=badass-heroine">badass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=broken-soul">broken-soul</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1142719608" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3699756381823842850"><b> “4.75 <i>forever</i> and <i>everything</i> stars”</b><br/><br/>Honestly, I was not happy with the story line, sudden appearance of an unknown foe and the need for vengeance after so many years didn't feel right. For nearly 50% of the story all that happening was the civil conversation between the characters or revisiting their past or professing their love. I was pretty much disappointment with it since this is not the usual way tiffany writes the story. It’s like she was trying very hard to give a closure to everyone and</span>
  <span id="freeText3699756381823842850" style="display:none"><b> “4.75 <i>forever</i> and <i>everything</i> stars”</b><br><br>Honestly, I was not happy with the story line, sudden appearance of an unknown foe and the need for vengeance after so many years didn't feel right. For nearly 50% of the story all that happening was the civil conversation between the characters or revisiting their past or professing their love. I was pretty much disappointment with it since this is not the usual way tiffany writes the story. It’s like she was trying very hard to give a closure to everyone and it was convenient to bring all the prime characters to sit and have a nice long chat and clear their misunderstanding or enlighten them with a story, I already predicted who is going to end up with whom and who will be left heartbroken. <i>(I know I was li’l judgy but blame the author for setting the standards so high in very passing book!)</i><br><br>But…what I didn’t expect was to live every bit of the stories told by <b>Søren, Nora and Kingsley</b>. The story about their past encounters the reason they love unconditionally was something so spectacular I felt it in my very core. Reading the previous books left me confused about Nora and Søren’s relationship, I never got to see why is that they need each other or why they find their way back to each other and those answers I found it here.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Sometimes only way to show someone <br>you love them is to let them go.”<i></i></i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Søren loved Nora for 20 years who in her very young age made him take his oath of celibacy back, who had a tendency to fall in trouble every chance she got. Took her under his wing, protected her, made her a strong independent woman and gave her his every wisdom but couldn’t give her a happily ever after. His heart loved her but his conscience wanted to set her free so that she could find somebody who isn’t worried to declare their love or worry about seeing together or atleast who would give her a family. Every time he sets her free every time she ran from him towards her freedom she never could deny the fact nobody loves her the way Søren did and that she always belonged to him.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Why do you love me so much, you stupid man?”<br>He smiled down at her. <br>“Because I met you.”<b></b></i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Those two were so imperfect yet perfect for each other. Let it be their open relationship, her need for dalliance, they never tried to change each other but accept it with open heart. Even with so many lovers who could buy her happiness she preferred being a priest’s <b>MISTRESS</b> rather than somebody’s wife. That’s something so tragically beautiful and best love story I’ve ever heard since forever. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I knelt at his feet because <br>I felt like that’s where I belonged. <br>And no, not because I was so unworthy of him, <br>but because he was so utterly worthy of my devotion.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>I’m glad that I was so wrong about Søren from beginning because seeing him from Nora’s eyes and listening him talk about her made me realized the prince charming and the damsel in despair need not be a normal people with perfect life but just two irrevocably loving, forgiving heart without expecting anything in return. All I want to say is-<b>you have not seen true love until you have met Søren and his Eleanor</b>. <br><br><b>Tiffany Reisz</b>-I don’t know what to say which hasn’t been said about this god’s most wonderful creation. Thank you…. for writing this magnificent series, for making me question my morals and ethics, for giving life to this characters who permanently reside in my heart, for showing different shades of love and for making me say when I find myself in a difficult situation <b>“What would Nora do?”</b>…Just <b>THANK YOU</b><br><br>It’s been literally 10 days since I met them; Their story sucked me in from the very beginning, I loved, loathed, laughed, swooned, prayed and cried over these characters. I couldn’t stop thinking about them when I’m awake, I dream (good and bad) about them, lost my sleep, lost my appetite, almost got fired for taking longer breaks during work hours BUT I don’t regret single minute of it. I promised myself I wouldn’t cry when I write this review but I cant help it, <i>*sobs*</i> it’s damn hard to say goodbye to them.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419939155ra/13148918.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>BTW the only reason I couldn’t give perfect 5 stars is <b>Grace</b>!!<br><br><i>Buddy read with my bestie Eda♥<br><br>P.S: One of the reason this series remain as an unforgettable memory is because I read it with you. Loved the banters, bitching about MC’s, swooning over King, rooting for our favorite couple and mostly loved that you were equally crazy about this series as I was. Thank you for being you! <br><br>P.P.S: Stop running after every silver Rolls Royce you see, King is too good to be true but if at all you find him....GIVE HIM MY NUMBER!!!! </i></span>
  <a data-text-id="3699756381823842850" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer471415184" class="readable"
